6a1(1): can thams cad la phan pa dang / bde ba'i don gyi phyir sems can gyi log par lta ba'i zug rngurtsa nas 'don pa'i phyir/ sems thegam pa'i byang chub sems dpa' dag byang chun
6a2(1): sems las phyir mi ldog cing brtan par bya ba'i phyir/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad thar phyin pa'i theg pa gcig gis lam la dgod pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po rnams
6a3(1): myur du mngon par byang chub cing sangs rgyas kyi drin lan byas pa'i phyir sems can thams cad kyis drin lji bar bya ba'i phyir// sems can thams cad kyis drin lci bar bya ba'i phyir/ sems can thams
6a4(1): tshod sdug bsngal gyi rgya mtsho las 'grol ba'i phyir/ so so'i skye bo mtha' dag pa ma la sri zhu bya bar 'dong ba'i phyir/ mdo 'di snang bar gyur pa yin no// de'i tshe 'khor de'i nang na byang chub sems dpa'
6a5(1): 'khor mang po'i gtso bo dang / ston par gyur pa stong phrag bcu snyed sngar las langs te/ bla gos phrogs cig tu byas nas/ pus me g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la gzugs/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di ska ces
6a6(1): gsol to// bcom ldan 'das kyis phrin gyis brnams kyis bdag cag rnams mi mjed kyi 'jig rten khams der mchi zhing / de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa la/ mchod pa dang bsnyen pakur bgyi ba dang / 
6a7(1): thabs mkhas pa chen po dang / sangs rgyas drin lan bsab pa'i mdo ba pa/ nyan cing mchi ba byin gyis brlabs du gsol/ de nas sangs rgyas des byang chub sems dpa' de rnams la 'di skad ces bas
6b1(1): stsal to// rigs kyi bu dag khyad mi mdzad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams der phrin na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de la la chad cing bkur sa bra ba dang / shin tu zang par dka' ba'i 'dushes 'asgreng bar dra na/ 
6b2(1): ci'i phyir zhe na/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa ni bskal ba grangs med pa bye ba khrag khrig gi bar du shin tu spyad de/ snying rje chen po'i smon lam 'di skad ces btab bo// gal te mngon par sangs rgyas pan/ 'dzin rte
6b3(1): gyi khams sdig pa can ri dang shang shong dang / gyo mo dang / gseg pa dang / cher ma la sogs pa'i gnas su sems can dag kyang nyon mongs pa dang bcas/ mtshams med pa lnga dang / mi dge ba bcu rdzogs par slo
6b4(1): pa'i gnas der mngon par sangs rgyas te/ phan pa dang / bde ba'i don du sdug bsngal thams cad yongs su ldan par byas nas/ chos kyi sku yongs su rdzogs shing / lhag ma ma lus pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa
6b5(1): gyur cig ces smon lam du btab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das des thog ma de skad ces smon lam btab pas/ khyed rnams 'jig rten gyi khams der phyir nas/ ji ltar sangs rgyas nyid gshegs pa dang / 
6b6(1): ji ltar sangs rgyas nyid bzhugs pa dang / 'dra bar gnas par bya'o// zhes bka' stsal pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyi tshig mthur par/ bcom ldan 'das kyi bka' bzhin du brgyam
6b7(1): shes gas lanas/ byang drub sems dpa' di dag re re yang 'khor bung chub sems dpa' bye ba khrig khrig brgya phreng snyeng gi yongs su bskur te/ mi mdzod kyi 'ji gnyen gyi khams gangan bdar sa dang // das
7a1(1): 'jig rten gyi khams dang gang du phyin par 'jig rten gyi khams de dag rnam pa drug du g.yos te/ 'od zer chen pos kun tu snang bar gyur/ steng gi bar snang las lha rnams kyis me tog
7a2(1): man+dAr dang / man+dAr chen po yang char bzhin du bab po// 'od gzer chen pos snang bar byas shing / rdzu 'phrul gyis 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dag kyang g.yos so// de ma yin pa
7a3(1): gzhan yang lha rdzas kyi rol mo tshad med pa brgya stong snyed kyis kyang / steng gi bar snang lam dkrol bar rang bzer bzhin du/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag bya rgo phung po'i rig la bder/ de bzhin
7a4(1): gshegs pa'i spyan sngar lhags nas/ zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ sangs rgyas la lan gsum bskor ba byas nas phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de'i tshe de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od gzer
7a5(1): gyis nub phyogs logs su sangs rgyas kyi zhing chad med pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong 'das pa'i pha rol tu 'jig rten gyi khams dag pa'i gnas zhes bya bar snang bar byas so// 'jig rten gyi kham
7a6(1): de na sangs rgyas kyi mtshan nyid ci tha mar pa'i 'od ces bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa dgra pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa 'de bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten
7a7(1): mkhyen pa skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo sbyar ba/ blan med pa son pa rgyal ba sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'de ba can zhes bu ban gzhugs te/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing dam bzhin
7b1(1): mnyam zhing bcur las byas pa/ gser ba rtsams thig zung gyis pa/ rin pa chen btu rgya gang bskyed sa/ gang de dag kyang mda' brgyang tsam du ma thob/ me tho ga nga 'bras bla nga ma na
7b2(1): mas shin tu brgyan pa/ rlung mi drag pa'i bskyod pas sgra snyan pa 'byung ba/ sgra de dag so so'i skye bos zos pa mi ngoms pa/ skabs skabs na chu mig dang / mtshe'u dang / khrus kyi rdzing bu yod la/ yon
7b3(1): brgyad dang ldan pa'i chus yongs su gang zhing / rdzing gi zhabs kyang gser gyi bye ma brdal ba/ rdzing gi dngos bzhin gsung dam pa dang ldan pa'i me tog dam pa dang / puN+Da rI ka dang / pa rI sha ka dang / de/ 
7b4(1): ma yin pa me tog sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po shing rta'i 'phang lo tsam chu'i yongs su khebs te/ chu'i nang na yang bya rnam pa sna tshogs kyang shin yid du 'ong ba'i sgra snyan pa byin
7b5(1): te/ rdzing de'i nang rin po che sna bdun las byas pa'i gru yod do// de na sems can mang po 'dod dgur rtse zhing longs spyod do// rin po che'i shing de dag gi bar na seng ge'i khri mtho khyad kyi chad dpag tshad
7b6(1): cig pa bshams nas/ rin po che sna bdun gyis brgyan pa/ lha rdzas kyi na bza' khri'i steng du rim par bting ba/ lha rdzas kyi spos kyi dri 'thul ba/ lha rdzas kyi me tog gis chal par bkram pa'i khri de la/ 
7b7(1): de bzhin gshegs pa nyi zla mar me 'od skyil mo krung bcas shing bzhugs pa la/ byang chub sems dpa' tshad med bye ba brgya stong snyed mdun du bdar te/ thal mo sbyar ba btung nas de bzhin gshes
8a1(1): pa de la so so nas tshig mthun par 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ci'i rgyu ci'i rkyen gyis 'od bzang po// kha dog sngon po dang / ser po dang / dbar po dang / dkar ba/ 
8a2(1): dang / bcas par ldan pa/ rab tu gsal ba dper mi bzod pa 'di/ shar phyogs nas 'khor mang po 'di dag la snang bar gyur te/ gang la 'od kyis reg pa de dag thams cad lus dang sems
8a3(1): bde bar gyur pa/ thugs brtse ba'i slad du bcom ldan 'das kyis bstan du gsol/ de la bcom ldan 'das des 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu dag legs par nyon la shin tu
8a4(1): yid la legs par bzung shig dang / khyed la grol bar bshad par bya'o// 'di nas shar phyogs logs su 'jig rten gyi khams tshad med pa zla ba khrag khrig brgya snyeng 'das pa'i pha rol na/ 
8a5(1): rgyas kyi zhing mi mjed ces bya ba yod do// de na sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa/ bde bar
8a6(1): gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba kha lo sbyor ba/ bla na med pa sbyin pa rgyal ba sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das zhes bya ba/ 'khor mang pos yongs su bskor nas/ 'kha
8a7(1): mang po thams cad la thabs mkhas mtshon pos zin lan bas pa pa'i mdo sde ston cing / sems can thams cad la len pa bde ba'i don gyi phyir sems can thams cad kyi log par lta ban
8b1(1): zug rngu ca nas 'don pa'i phyir/ sems thog ma'i byang chub sems dpa' dag byang chub las phyir mi ldog cing bstan par bya ba'i phyir/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad mthar smin
8b2(1): pa'i theg pa gcig gi lam la dgod pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams myur du mngon par byang chub cing / sangs rgyas kyi drin lan bsang pa'i phyir/ sems
8b3(1): thams cad kyi drin lan lnga badran par bya ba'i brir/ sems can thams cad sdug bsngal gyi rgya mtsho las bskal ba'i phyir/ ma sa'i skye bo dag pa la sri zhu bya bar 'dod pa'i phyir/ mdo 'di
8b4(1): bar gyur pa yin no// de'i tshe 'khor byang chub sems dpa' 'khor mang pa'i gtso ba dang ston par gyur pa/ stong phrag bcu snyed stan lus blangs te/ bla gos phyogs gcig tu byas nas/ 
8b5(1): pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das kyis byin gyis brlabs kyis/ bdag cag rnams mi mdzad kyi 'jin
8b6(1): rten khams der mchis zhing / de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa la mchod pa dang / bsnyen bkur bgyi ba dang / thabs mkhas pa chen po sangs rgyas zin lan bsab pa'i mdo sde dam pa nyan cing
8b7(1): mchi bar byin gyis brlab du gsol to// de nas sangs rgyas nges byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu dag khyed mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams der phyin nas/ 
9a1(1): / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de la mchod cing bkur sti bya ba dang / shin tu phrad par dka' ba'i 'du shes bskyed par bya'o// de'i ci'i phyir zhe na/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa ni bam
9a2(1): ma grangs med pa bye ba khrag khrig gi bar du shin tu sprang dka' ba spyad de/ snying rje chen po'i smon lam 'di skad ces btab po// gal te mngon par sangs rgyas pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams sdig pa can ri dang
9a3(1): shang shong dang / gyo mo dang / gseg ma dang / tsher ma la sogs yod pa'i gnas su/ sems can dag kyang nyon mongs pa dang bcas pa/ mtshams med pa lnga dang / mi dge ba bcu tshogs par spyod pa/ 
9a4(1): gnas der sangs rgyas te/ phan pa dang bde ba'i don du sdug bsngal thams cad yongs su bcad de/ bde ba thams cad dang ldan par byas nas/ chos kyi sku yongs su rdzogs shing lhag ma ma lus
9a5(1): pa'i mya ngan 'das par gyur cig ces smon lam btab po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das des thog ma de skad ces smon lam btab pa/ khyed rnams 'jig rten gyi khams der phyin nas/ ji ltar sangs
9a6(1): rgyas nyid bzhugs pa dang 'dra bar gnas par bya'o zhes bka' stsal pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyi tshig mthun par/ bcom ldan 'das kyi bka' bzhin du bgyi'o// zhes
9a7(1): gsol nas/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag rer yang 'khor byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya stod kyis yongs su bskor te/ mi mdzad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gangan ba der mang / 
9b1(1): de dag 'jig rten gyi khams gang dang gang du phyin par/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag rnam pa drug du g.yos te/ 'od zer chen po yang kun tu snang bar gyur/ steng gi bar snang las lha rnams kyi me tog man+ta
9b2(1): ba dang / mthur ba chen po yang char bzhin du phab po// 'od gzer chen pos snang bar byas shing / rdzu 'phrul gyis 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi/ bye ma sdeng dag kyang g.yas so// de ma yin pa kanan
9b3(1): yang lha rdzas kyi rol mchod med pa brgya stong snyed kyang steng gyi bar snang lam dkrol bar rang zer ba bzhin du/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag bye rgod spungs pa'i rig la bder/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan sngar
9b4(1): lpags te zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ sangs rgyas la len gsum bskor ba byas nas phyogs gcig tu 'khod // de'i tshe de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas/ kha dog rnams lnga dang ldan pa'i rdong
9b5(1): zer gyis byang phyogs su sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig lnga brgya 'das pa'i pha rol na/ 'jig rten gyi khams dbang phyug grags pa'i rgyal po zhes bya ba snang bar byas so// 'jig rten gyi khams de na sangs
9b6(1): rgyas pad+mo la rgan gyi 'od ces bya ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang nabs su ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs pa 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul
9b7(1): ba'i kha lo sgyur ba/ bla na med pa/ ston pa rgyal ba sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi zhing dri ma dang bral ba zhes pan bzhugs te/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing de yang shin tu mnyam zhing gni bai DUrar+ya las
10a1(1): / byas pa/ gser btso ma'i thig les bris pa/ rin po che sna bdun gyi shing skye ba shing de dag kyang mda' rgyang tsam du zad pa/ me tog dang 'bras bu dang / yal ga dang 'dab mas shin
10a2(1): tu brgyad pa/ rlung mi drag pas bskyod ra sgra snyan pa byung ba/ sgra de dag kyang so so'i skye bos thos na mi ngoms pa/ skabs skabs na chu mig dang mche'u dang / khrus kyi rdzing bu yod la/ yon tan brgyad
10a3(1): dang ldan pa'i chus yongs su gang zhing / rdzing gi zhabs kyang gser gi bye mas brdal ba/ rdzing gi ngos bzhin gsung dam pa dang ldan pa'i me tog pad+ma dang / puN+Da rI ka dang / pa ri sha ka dang / des
10a4(1): yin pa'i me tog sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po shing rta'i pang lo tsam chu'i steng yongs su khyebs te/ chu'i nang na bya sna tshogs yang shin tu yid du 'ong ba'i sgra snyan pa 'byin
10a5(1): to// rdzing de'i ning na rin po che sna bdun las byas pa'i gru yod de/ de na sems can mang po bdod dgur rtse zhing longs spyod do// rin po che'i shing de dag gi bar bar na/ seng ge'i khrimatho/ 
10a6(1): khyad dpag tshad gcig pa bshams nas/ rin po che sna bdun gyis brgyan te/ lha rdzas kyi na bza' khri'i steng rim par bting ba/ spos kyi dri 'thul ba/ lha rdzas kyi me tog gis chal par
10a7(1): ba lam pa'i khri'i thig na/ de bzhin gshegs pa pad+mo le rgan gyi 'od chags pa/ skyil mo krung du bcas shing bzhugs pa la/ byang chub sems dpa' tshang med pa'i bye ba brgya srong snyed mdun / 
10b1(1): bdang te/ thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa de la so so nas tshig mthun par 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ci'i rgyu ci'i rkyen gyis 'od bzang po kha dog ldan pa
10b2(1): dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po dang / ldan pa rab tu gsal ba dper mi bzod pa 'di/ lho phyogs logs nas/ 'khor mang po 'di dag la snang bar 'gyur te/ gang la 'ong
10b3(1): reg pa de dag thams cad lus dang sems bde bar 'gyur ba/ thugs brtse ba'i slad du bcom ldan 'das kyis bstan du gsol/ de la bcom ldan 'das des 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu
10b4(1): dag legs par nyon la yid la legs par bzung shig dang / khyed la dkrol zhing bshad par bya'o// 'di nas lho phyogs logs su/ 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba khrag brgya stong 'das pa'i pha rol na/ 
10b5(1): sangs rgyas kyi zhing ma mjed ces bya ba yod de/ de nas sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa/ 
10b6(1): bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo sgyur ba/ bla na med pa ston rgyal ba sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das zhes bya ba 'khor mang pos yongs su bskor nas// 
10b7(1): 'khor mang po thams cad la thabs mkhas pa chen po rngon lan bsab pa'i mdo sde ston cing sems can thams cad la phan pa dang / bde ba'i don gyi phyir/ sems can thams cad kyi log
11a1(1): par lta ba'i zug rngus nas 'don pa'i phyir/ sems thog ma pa'i byang chub sems dpa' dag byang chub las phyir mi ldog cing / banan par bya ba'i phyir/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas
11a2(1): thams cad mthar phyin pa'i theg pa gcig la dgod pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams byung du mngon par byang chub cing / sangs rgyasadzin lan bslab pa'i phyir/ sems
11a3(1): can thams cad kyi drin lan lci bar dran bya ba'i phyir/ sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyi rgya mtsho las sbrel ba'i phyir/ so so'i skye bo dag pa la srid zhu bya bar 'dod pa'i phyir/ mdo 'di snang bar
11a4(1): 'gyur ba yin no// de'i tshe 'khor mang po'i nang na byang chub sems dpa' 'khor mang po'i gtso bo dang / ston par gyur pa/ stong phrag bcu snyed stan las langs par gyur nas/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu byas
11a5(1): nas/ pus ma g.yas pa'i lpangs la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das de la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis/ bdag cag rnams mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi kham
11a6(1): der mchi zhing / der de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa la mchod pa dang bsrer bkur bgyi ba dang / thabs mkhas pa chen po sangs rgyas drin lan bsapa pa'i mdo sbe ma pa can cing mchi bar byin gyis brla ba rdugasapa
11a7(1): na sa sangs rgyas des byang chub sems dpa' rnams la 'di skad ces bka' bul to// rigs kyi bung ga khyed mdzad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams de byin na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das del mtshang cing ba sa
11b1(1): bya ba dang / shin tu phrad dka' ba'i 'du shes bskyed par bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa ni bskal pa grangs med pa bye ba khrag khrig gi bar du/ shin tu spyod dka' ba spyad pas snying rje chen po'i
11b2(1): smon lam 'di skad ces btab bo// gal te mngon par sangs rgyas pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams sdig pa can ri dang shang shong dang / gyo mo dang bsag pa dang / tsher ma la sogs yod pa'i gnas su/ sems can dang / 
11b3(1): kyang nyin mongs pa dang bcas pa/ mtshams med pa lnga dang / mi dge ba bcu rdzogs par spyad pa'i gnas der mngon par sangs rgyas te/ phan pa dang bde ba'i dor du sdug bsngal thams cad yongs su bca // 
11b4(1): ba thams cad dang ldan par byas nas/ chos kyi sku yongs su rdzogs shing lhag ma ma lus pa'i mya ngan las 'das par gyur cig ces smon lam bzhab po// sangs rgyas nges thog ma de sad ces smon lam btab
11b5(1): pas khyed rnams 'jig rten gyi khams der phyin nas/ ji ltar sangs rgyas nyid gshegs pa dang / ji ltar sangs rgyas nyid bzhugs pa dang 'dra bar gnas par bya'o// zhes bka' stsal pa dang / byang chub
11b6(1): sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyis tshig mthun par/ bcom ldan 'das kyi bka' bzhin du bgyi'o zhes gsol nas/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag re re yang 'khor byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig
11b7(1): brgya stong snyed kyis yongs su bskor te/ mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang na ba der song ste/ de dag 'jig rten gyi khams gang dang gang du phyin par 'jig rten gyi khams de dag rnam par drug tu g.yos te/ 'od zer
12a1(1): rten pa mang can sa ba rnam shing gib slang las rnams byas mtha / mdur bachen pa mngar bzhi du bab// 'dag zer chen po ma snang ba ma pa rdul
12a2(1): 'di kyi sa skyes kyang gams sa// des man gzhan yang grangs kyis pa ra med pa skyed pa/ meng gib spangs mang bras pa dang zer nas byang ba sa
12a3(1): dag ca ni grungs pa'i dzin pa de brji gas pa'i kun snang lpags nas/ nabs lamag pas brag 'tshal te/ sangs rgyas la lan gsum bskor ba zlas nas grags gcig dul ba dang // 
12a4(1): du phyogs mtshams pani dang / snying nga yin go zugs dang / bregs bcunas gags pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pa thams cad kyis/ ses nas 'khor brgya snang grangs ma pa
12a5(1): dang bcas te/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der lhags nas/ mchod pa dang / bkur stir byas/ bstod ma byas nas/ thams cad kyis mgrin gcig tu tshigs su bcad brgya stong snyed kyis/ bcom ldan
12a6(1): 'das la yongs su papa da// de ltar sangs rgyas la bskrad pa nas kyang brags gcig tu la la // de'i chi mi midzad kyi' rig rten gyi khams kyang yongs su dag par gyur te/ de ze dang / ra
12a7(1): dang / ri chung ngu dang / gtsang ba dang / chu rlung dang / mche'u dang / rdzing dang / ldeng ka dang / gang shong dang / ngam grogs med cing / den gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyang 'od kyis snang bar byas / 
12b1(1): sangs rgyas gangan ba der lhags te/ dga' zhing mgu ba'i sems kyis thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ mig mi 'dzums par chags pa'i yid kyis lta zhing 'khod do// de nas bcom
12b2(1): ldan 'das kyis 'od zer phyir 'dus par mdzad de/ 'od zer de dag gis sku la lan bdun bskor nas dbu ka'i bcug tu nub par gyur te/ de ltar gyur pa kun blos mthong nas/ 'khor mang po thams cad kyang rje
12b3(1): chom du gyur par sems kyis rab tu shes pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mdzad pa thabs mkhas pa mngon par bstan pa dang / phyis ma 'ongs pa'i skye bo dag gis shes rab kyi mig dbye ba dang / so so'i skye bo
12b4(1): thams cad sred pa'i chu klung las brgal zhing pha rol tu phyin pas bde ba la bkod pa dang / so so'i skye bo dag pa me dang / slob dpon dang / bla ma'i drin lci ba dran zhing shes pa bya ba'i phyir stan las langs nas/ gos tshags
